<text>I always try the carne asada (steak) burrito when ever I try a new Mexican Restaurant, it's my standard benchmark. This was the best carne asada burrito I've had in a very long time. The burrito is without frills (which is awesome), and you can taste the quality of the fresh ingredients they use, the flavor is like mom's cooking.

This is a small place, but don't let the cozy atmosphere fool you. The owner is warm and welcoming.

The food is excellent. The chips were fresh, salsa was good, and they had nopales (cactus salsa) which is a sure sign of being a legit Mexican Restaurant.

Dangerously close to addiction, I see myself visiting this Mexican restaurant a couple times a week.

If your jaded from the same 'ol burritos, give them a try. I highly recommend this place.<//text>< Pictures>

< gmap_id>
0x80940cf3df55bcd5:0x9a79729fd9564bc< /gmap_id>
<Date>1530847168295</Date>< Review>
This is not a pet store. They are a shelter run off of donations and what little bit they get from the county. Do not expect a pet store when you go here to find your new family member!
We got our guy, named by the shelter Hunk of Love, renamed by us as Kona a month ago. He came home with tapeworms and hookworms, as well as a bad case of kennel cough. He had been seen by their vet and we weren't told he had any of those things, but only so much can be accomplished by a skeleton crew of people and no money to hire more help.
Don't adopt a dog unless you can care for it, and don't expect to not have to pay some money to get your pup up to perfect health. But don't let that deter you--if you care about animals and are truly invested in your love of them you will make the choice to support this shelter and adopt.
TL;DR: Despite the vet costs after adoption, my family and I couldn't be happier with our new addition!<//Review>

<Text>My partner and I came in from out of town and loved the idea of cycling through Joshua Tree, but didn't have a way of bringing bikes with us. We're so happy to have found JTree Bike Shop. They offer fat tire bicycle rentals for desert riding, and will even give you a lift uphill to the Section 6 Desert View Conservation Area trails where you can bike through some pretty amazing stuff. We were treated with great hospitality and got to hear some history and information about Joshua Tree from an employee who'd lived there most of his life. You're given water, helmets, a map, a bike pump, some basic tools and tube-mounted bags to keep you going. We ended up staying out for about 4 hours; though we could have gone longer. There's definitely some technical cycling required, but the trails are well-maintained and have been traveled by the shop. The day cost us each $70, which is spendy, but left us with some of the best memories of our trip. Worth it.<//Text>< Pictures>

I bought a new house in a nice neighborhood and wanted to have a good pest control service to keep the bugs at bay.  Jake was going door to door and did a house evaluation.  He was able to point out areas of concern and even found a number of black widows with egg sacks.  The initial price was $129 per quarter for complete treatment with unlimited retreats for free. We went over all my areas of concern with fleas, flies, mosquitoes, silver fish and gnats.  The first service was good, the tech seemed to know what he was doing and was professional. My only complaint was that the tech was not able to fully treat my Ivy wall as I specifically asked Jake about.  He said that the sales guys are from Utah and dont know California regulations.  Apparently they arent allowed to treat anything over 4 feet.  SO if i have an 8' tall green wall that is bug and spider central, they cant treat it.   Over the course of the month after the treatment I noticed a significant increase in bug activity.  I called.  It took 4 calls and then be put on a call back list to talk to someone.   The service tech came, at an unannounced time, far after the scheduled appointment.  He then said that my watering was the problem. Now I am not a bug specialist, but I water 5 minutes at a shot 4 days/week.  That doesn't seem like a lot.  I also have it set to manual mode, so the sprinklers are not going off without my knowledge.  I am not over watering.  Then to my suprise, he hands me another $129 bill.  he said because its the start of a new quarter, there is another charge.  My first treatment was in June.  They apparently go by calendar quarter not start of service.  I got on the phone with customer service again (took four days to get a call back) and the customer service person proceeds to tell me they dont treat for Gnats and the standard treatment i am paying for only covers a 3 foot perimeter around the house. Full yard treatment is more under an additional service contract.   They are misrepresenting their service capabilities, and treatment methods.  Do not use this service. I am back to Pacific Pest control I used at another house.</review>

<time>1592597434876< /time><Rating>1<//Rating>< review>
DO NOT FALL FOR THIS. They have very persuasive and pushy sales people that will stop at nothing to get you to sign the contract and pay right away. They will result to guilt tactics and seemingly give you "special and exclusive discounts" if you sign up right away. They know people are going to push back so they've hiked their prices up in order to "discount" them in front of you to hook you into signing a very long and deceptive contract.

*If you've already signed the contract, then YOU HAVE 3 BUSINESS DAYS TO CANCEL WITHOUT PENALTY otherwise you'll be charged a hefty $249-$349 cancellation fee. Make sure to sign and date Page 3 of the contract (the page that says "Notice of Cancellation" at the top) and email it or drop it off in person within 3 business days of signing the contract.

By the way, the sales person did not mention the contract cancellation fee until I kept digging and asking more questions. Finally they said they'd knock it down from $349 to $200. After the sales person left, I read the contract and it had $249 listed as a cancellation fee. Super DECEPTIVE. *Read the contract before you sign anything.*

Also, they should not be sending Sales people DOOR to DOOR during the CORONAVIRUS pandemic. It is NOT over yet. There are spikes in cases every day and most of the houses in my neighborhood they are pitching to are elderly and at risk. This is horrible business practice. Also the sales person was not wearing a mask.

This review is NOT a review on their actual service. I cannot attest to whether or not it is quality or worth the price. However, even if the services were good, there are plenty of other decent pest control companies with honest and upfront business practices and pricing. Based on their sales tactics alone, I cannot recommend Aptiv at all.</review>
